2026-02-15T21:31:04.8232794Z │             0.5 * (1.0 + tanh((y - 0.75) / sigma))
2026-02-15T21:31:04.8233041Z │     )
2026-02-15T21:31:04.8233317Z │     # Sinusoidal perturbation in vy to seed the instability
2026-02-15T21:31:04.8233651Z │     vy = A_pert * sin(4 * pi * x)
2026-02-15T21:31:04.8233932Z │     return SVector(rho, vx_smooth, vy, P0)
2026-02-15T21:31:04.8234172Z │ end
